# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="43589-102">.NET Framework 中過時的類型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="43589-103">本文中的表格列出 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 和 [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)] 中過時的類型，並依組件分組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="43589-104">使用下列連結查看每個組件中過時的型別和建議的替代方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="43589-105">因為這些型別已經過時，其所有成員也已經過時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="43589-106">如需 .NET Framework 類別庫中其他過時成員的清單，請參閱[過時的成員](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_system_assemblies"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-types-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="43589-133">系統組件中的過時型別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-133">Obsolete Types in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="43589-134">下列表格將列出已經在系統組件中宣告為過時的型別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-134">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="43589-135">這些組件是用於以 .NET Framework 為目標的一般用途應用程式開發。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-135">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_microsoft_assemblies"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-types-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="43589-925">Microsoft 組件中的過時型別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-925">Obsolete Types in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="43589-926">下列章節將列出 Microsoft 組件中的過時型別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-926">The following sections list the obsolete types in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="43589-927">這些組件是特殊用途的組件，例如以個別語言 (例如 Microsoft.JScript.dll 或 Microsoft.VisualC.dll) 為目標的組件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-927">These assemblies are special-purpose assemblies such as assemblies that target an individual language (for example, Microsoft.JScript.dll or Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span></span>  
  
<a name="IEHost"></a>   
### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="43589-928">組件：IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-928">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="43589-929">IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe 組件已經從 .NET Framework 中移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-929">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="43589-930">其所有型別和成員都已經過時，而且 [!INCLUDE[net_v40_short](../../../includes/net-v40-short-md.md)] 中不再支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-930">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported as of the [!INCLUDE[net_v40_short](../../../includes/net-v40-short-md.md)].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="43589-931">這些組件之前是用來裝載 Windows Form 控制項以及在 Internet Explorer 中執行可執行檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-931">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="43589-932">建議的替代方案包括 ClickOnce、XAML 瀏覽器應用程式 (XBAP) 和 Microsoft Silverlight。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="43589-932">Recommended alternatives include ClickOnce, XAML browser applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
